 1309 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      2 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08EF               | * Create_Sprite — Compiled sprite engine

 1311 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      4 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08EF               | *
 1312 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      5 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08EF               | * Compiles shape data into native 65816 code that
 1313 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      6 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08EF               | * draws sprites via direct-page writes to SHR shadow RAM.
 1314 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      7 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08EF               | *
 1315 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      8 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08EF               | * Call: copy sprite table ($18 bytes) to bank $00 direct page,
 1316 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      9 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08EF               | *       LDA #dp_address / JSR Create_Sprite
 1317 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     10 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08EF               | *
 1318 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     11 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08EF               | * Sprite table format (24 bytes at DP offsets $00-$17):
 1319 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     12 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08EF               | *   $00 ADRL Rout_Adr    — output: where compiled code is written
 1320 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     13 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08EF               | *   $04 ADRL Shape_Adr   — input: shape pixel data (24-bit)
 1321 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     14 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08EF               | *   $08 ADRL Msk_Adr     — $000000=none, $FFFF00=auto, $FEFE00=decor
 1322 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     15 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08EF               | *   $0C DA   Tbl_Nb      — TABLE_ROUT index (updated by routine)
 1323 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     16 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08EF               | *   $0E DA   Nb_Lgn      — bytes per shape row
 1324 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     17 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08EF               | *   $10 DA   Nb_Col      — bytes per shape column
 1325 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     18 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08EF               | *   $12 DA   Lgn         — row ($FFFF=dynamic via Y register)
 1326 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     19 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08EF               | *   $14 DA   Col         — column
 1327 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     20 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08EF               | *   $16 DA   Pixel_Shape — $00=no sub-pixel, $01=half-pixel shift
